posted:Posted March 24, 2024
msg:I highly recommend this hotel. Firstly the swimming pool is the best hotel swimming pool I've ever used. It is long, easily 20-25 metres and also wide, but shallow with no deep water. Perfect for relaxing lap swimming. And it is always supervised. One tip. You'll have to wear a swimming cap which they sell at the front desk of the swimming pool, so make sure you bring something to pay for it on your first swim.
Secondly, the hotel's location (on top of the Zhuzhianglu metro station) is perfect for getting to all the best places and attractions. And on cold days and hot days you can access the metro (press -2 in the lift) without having to deal with the weather.
Thirdly, the staff are amazing. Rachel, Brittany, William, Allen, could not do enough to help me during my stay.
Lastly, the shops and restaurants in the two basement levels offer a level of convenience that I have not received anywhere else that I have stayed. I was able to buy all essentials and have delicious Chinese food, incredibly affordably and conveniently.

msg:Spring is the best time to travel to Nanjing. Although I only stayed at Golden Eagle Pearl River No. 1 for two days, the time was very short, but I felt very good.
The hotel is located in the city center with super convenient transportation. It is just at Exit 4 of Zhujiang Station on Metro Line 1. The first to sixth floors of the ground floor are shopping centers and catering gathering places. The seventh floor is the hotel, which can solve shopping, dining, shopping and accommodation. You can basically take the subway to the scenic spots. The best thing is that you don‚Äôt have to worry about traffic jams when you leave.
The service staff are very friendly and enthusiastic. Whether they meet in the lobby or the corridor, they will take the initiative to say hello.
The breakfast is very rich, with both Chinese and Western styles, and the choice is strong. The restaurant environment is very comfortable.
The room was upgraded to a suite. The bedding and bath towels are clean and refreshing. The bathroom is clean, dry and wet are separated, and the shower is very smooth. This is especially great.
A small suggestion: it is better to add a night light to the bathroom, otherwise the corridor light needs to be turned on at night. However, this small problem will not affect the five-point praise. I will choose to stay here next time I go to Nanjing.
